Video Description: The Arabs and the Zionists in Palestine struggle to get their bearings in a ruined world. The smell of gunsmoke still lays thick over the landscape, and the ink is still wet on the Balfour Declaration and the several new international agreements. The First World War is over, and people around the world are demanding their independence in the new world order. But building a national identity takes more than just drawing lines on a map or running a rag up a flagpole.

*  See, modern industrial capitalism functions best when people can be packed up and transported to wherever the great industrial machine happens to need them at any given time. [[01:55:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=6926.7s)]
*  It's an obstacle to efficiency if people are too attached to a place. [[01:55:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=6936.7s)]
*  If your whole family, going back three generations and stretching out to the second and third cousins, all live in a 40 mile radius and they've done so for years, [[01:55:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=6941.7s)]
*  you're going to be much less likely to just pack up your little nuclear family and move across the country for another job. [[01:55:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=6950.7s)]
*  It's a much bigger decision than it would be in a place like the United States for example, where most likely you moved to the other side of the country as soon as you left home for college [[01:55:57](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=6957.7s)]

*  At the same time, another group began to gain prominence and this group would very soon come to dominate the entire movement. [[02:46:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=9985.7s)]
*  In the early days, I think we mentioned this once before, the Zionist community in Palestine was dominated by Jews from the Russian Empire. [[02:46:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=9992.7s)]
*  And they carried the same emphasis on leftist economics and class unity that was creating chaos in the old empire. [[02:46:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10001.7s)]
*  To a significant degree, these were the same people. [[02:46:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10007.7s)]
*  They moved back and forth sometimes between movements. [[02:46:50](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10010.7s)]
*  Now, for a while, they all came in several flavors, these leftist Zionists, from full-on communists to agrarian socialists to something like what we would think of today as social democrats. [[02:46:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10012.7s)]
*  But eventually all of those flavors would collapse into one as labor Zionism, largely due to the will and power of a man who arrived in Palestine in 1906 at 20 years old. [[02:47:03](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10023.7s)]
*  If you fly into the state of Israel today, chances are you'll be landing at the airport bearing his name, David Ben-Gurion. [[02:47:15](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10035.7s)]
*  David Ben-Gurion was born, David Green, in the Polish city of Plonsk, 200 miles from where Haim Wiseman was currently growing up. [[02:47:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10043.7s)]
*  He was 11 years old when Ben-Gurion was born. [[02:47:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10050.7s)]
*  And he's really the man who, for me and for most people, really captures what a Zionist in Palestine was. [[02:47:32](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10052.7s)]
*  And I say specifically in Palestine because as we go on, there are going to be Jews all over Europe and in Britain and the United States who were Zionists, committed Zionists, who were actively supporting the movement, doing work for it, dedicating themselves to it. [[02:47:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10061.7s)]
*  But they have a fundamentally different character than the Zionists that are in Palestine. [[02:47:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10074.7s)]
*  The Zionist project never could have gotten off the ground with these people without their fundraising and lobbying in Britain and the United States, for sure. [[02:48:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10080.7s)]
*  They were very important to the movement, but that was fundamentally different work than facing the daily realities of building the Jewish homeland in Palestine. [[02:48:06](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10086.7s)]
*  For that, you needed a different kind of Zionist. And Ben-Gurion fit the bill for it as if he'd been designed in a lab. [[02:48:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10096.7s)]
*  He's a short guy, maybe about five feet tall, an inch or two taller, but kind of stocky. [[02:48:22](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10102.7s)]
*  He's pugnacious. He's got this, he's just an ornery guy, very sure of himself. [[02:48:28](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10108.7s)]
*  He just does not let people get in his way, though. He seems to have unlimited energy. [[02:48:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10114.7s)]
*  When he arrived in Palestine, he has a full head of hair, but very quickly he went bald. [[02:48:39](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10119.7s)]
*  And he's more remembered for having a shiny bald head with just two ridiculous white tufts of hair exploding out from each side above his ears. [[02:48:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10123.7s)]
*  You just imagine a short, stocky guy scowling as much as you can possibly screw up your face with a shiny bald head and two giant tufts of white hair exploding above your ears. [[02:48:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10132.7s)]
*  That's Ben-Gurion. [[02:49:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10142.7s)]
*  Now, Ben-Gurion's socialist Zionism drew on the same kind of vulgar romantic ideas that were popular in Central Europe in the early part of the 20th century. [[02:49:04](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10144.7s)]
*  He was a secular guy, but his ideas about the relationship of a people to a given spot of land were almost mystical. [[02:49:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10153.7s)]
*  He was obsessed with making the Negev Desert bloom. It was just his big idea. He never really succeeded at it. [[02:49:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10161.7s)]
*  But he believed that working the land was an act of fundamental value that was necessary for the drifting Jewish people to once again become rooted in their home. [[02:49:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10167.7s)]
*  So while Theodor Herzl was interested in creating a sort of bourgeois industrial state, and while Ahad Ham would have said that the diaspora should turn their hearts toward Jerusalem to pray, [[02:49:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10176.7s)]
*  Ben-Gurion would have said that if they want to be a Zionist, they should move to Jerusalem, pick up a shovel, and get to work. [[02:49:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10188.7s)]
*  Now, while David Ben-Gurion was not driven by the spiritual motives of Ahad Ham, I don't want to be mistaken. [[02:49:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10194.7s)]
*  He didn't settle for the reactionary political Zionism of Theodor Herzl necessarily either. [[02:50:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10200.7s)]
*  In fact, anti-Semitism didn't really play much of a role in Ben-Gurion's Zionism. [[02:50:05](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10205.7s)]
*  In his memoirs, he would later write, [[02:50:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10209.7s)]
*  Russians, Jews, and Poles. [[02:50:40](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10240.7s)]
*  The number of Jews and Poles in the city were roughly equal, about 5,000 each. [[02:50:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10242.7s)]
*  The Jews, however, formed a compact centralized group occupying the innermost district, while the Poles were more scattered, living in outlying areas and shading off into the peasantry. [[02:50:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10246.7s)]
*  Consequently, when a gang of Jewish boys met a Polish gang, the latter would almost inevitably represent just a single suburb, [[02:50:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10256.7s)]
*  and thus be poorer in fighting potential than the Jews, who, even if their numbers were initially fewer, could quickly call on reinforcements from the entire quarter. [[02:51:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10262.7s)]
*  Far from being afraid of them, they were rather afraid of us. [[02:51:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10270.7s)]
*  In general, however, relations were amicable, though distant. [[02:51:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10273.7s)]
*  So that's David Ben-Gurion for you. [[02:51:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10277.7s)]
*  He's telling you about his hometown, and he's sizing up the various communities' fighting potential. [[02:51:19](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10279.7s)]
*  That's what this guy is all about. [[02:51:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10284.7s)]
*  Before arriving in Palestine in 1906, he'd already been arrested twice for subversive activities during the 1905 Russian Revolution. [[02:51:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10287.7s)]
*  That was as a 19-year-old. [[02:51:34](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10294.7s)]
*  You get the idea when you read about him that if you decide to pick a fight with this guy, you better pack a lunch. [[02:51:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10296.7s)]
*  That's something that a lot of people, a lot of Arabs and British and even other Jews, are going to learn, and it's something that a lot of them are going to learn the hard way. [[02:51:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10303.7s)]
*  Now, Ben-Gurion's politics and economics, while he was a leftist, it always took a back seat to his Jewish nationalism. [[02:51:54](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10314.7s)]
*  A strict socialist preached class unity, but Ben-Gurion was, let's say, a nationalist first and a socialist second. [[02:52:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10321.7s)]
*  But in 1921, the Jewish left in Palestine was heterogeneous. [[02:52:09](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10329.7s)]
*  There were still all types of leftists. [[02:52:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10334.7s)]
*  There were hardcore elements aligned with the Russian revolutionaries who sought to create a Soviet Palestine. [[02:52:16](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10336.7s)]
*  And these often clashed with other Jewish groups as much as they clashed with the British or the Arabs. [[02:52:21](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10341.7s)]
*  Back in the first episode, I mentioned that Trotsky had attended some of the early Zionist meetings, but that he eventually rejected Zionism because he rejected nationalism, period. [[02:52:26](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10346.7s)]
*  The Bolshevists, especially back in 1921, they rejected all national identity. [[02:52:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10355.7s)]
*  They thought that that was just a way to keep the workers of the world divided and at each other's throats. [[02:52:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10362.7s)]
*  It was something that the elites used to divide people up and make them think that they have enemies and other workers in other countries, but the Bolshevists rejected all that. [[02:52:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10367.7s)]
*  There were Jewish communities in Palestine who had the same idea. [[02:52:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10375.7s)]
*  They would often pass out flyers in Arabic, telling poor Arabs not to be fooled by the false divisions of Arab, Jew, Christian, Muslim, and all that. [[02:52:59](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10379.7s)]
*  Arab workers and Jewish workers should be united in opposition to their oppressors, whether they be Jewish, Arab, or British. [[02:53:07](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10387.7s)]
*  This is the kind of anti-nationalism that brought the communists into conflict with every nationalist movement in Europe, and it did the same thing here in Palestine. [[02:53:14](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10394.7s)]
*  Despite often supporting more or less the same leftist economic policies, the Zionists saw the communists as a significant threat to their project. [[02:53:23](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10403.7s)]
*  They were trying to build a national Jewish identity, and here were a group of Jews saying that all national identity should be thrown out. [[02:53:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10413.7s)]
*  Ben-Gurion's labor Zionists had begun to militarize after the Nebbi-Musa riots, but it wasn't only the Arabs they were preparing to fight. [[02:53:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10422.7s)]
*  Clashes began to occur between the communists and Ben-Gurion's socialist, but nationalist labor Zionists. [[02:53:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10429.7s)]
*  It all came to a head about a year after the Nebbi-Musa riots. [[02:53:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10438.7s)]
*  On May 1st, 1921, the communists had been distributing flyers in Yiddish and Arabic, announcing their plans to establish a Soviet Palestine. [[02:54:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10442.7s)]
*  They also announced their intention to hold a march from the city of Jaffa to Tel Aviv to commemorate May Day. [[02:54:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10451.7s)]
*  A group of labor Zionists led by David Ben-Gurion organized a countermarch to confront the communists in the streets. [[02:54:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10457.7s)]
*  Ben-Gurion's group was well organized, and when they saw the communists the next morning, they attacked. [[02:54:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10464.7s)]
*  A huge fight ensues, and the British police rush in, but they're very quickly overwhelmed. There just aren't enough of them. [[02:54:29](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10469.7s)]
*  Muslim and Christian Arabs from the nearby neighborhoods take up sticks and go to help the police against a group of communists who have been pushed to a sand dune. [[02:54:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10476.7s)]
*  That fight grows into a huge riot, and just as it had during the Nebbi-Musa festival, the cry goes out that the Jews have come to attack the Arabs. [[02:54:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10483.7s)]
*  Within a few hours, violence in the city becomes general and soon spreads to nearby towns and villages. [[02:54:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10491.7s)]
*  Arabs took to the streets and attacked Jewish shops and homes, thinking that they were under attack. [[02:54:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10496.7s)]
*  Many innocent Jews were targeted, but the fact that there were actually organized Jewish militia units running the streets and retaliating against the Arabs seemed to reinforce this idea that there was a planned attack by the Jews. [[02:55:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10501.7s)]
*  As always in times of chaos, the worst of the worst seemed to find room to operate. [[02:55:12](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10512.7s)]
*  Jews who weren't even involved in the protest marches were set upon and killed by Arab gangs. [[02:55:20](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10520.7s)]
*  There's a story of a 14-year-old Jewish girl being chased down and beaten to death with iron rods. [[02:55:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10525.7s)]
*  Several women were raped and mutilated. Herbert Samuel called in reinforcements to attack the Arabs. [[02:55:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10530.7s)]
*  They used British gunboats and bombers and armored vehicles against the mobs, and British soldiers used machine guns and aircraft to fire into Arab crowds, [[02:55:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10536.7s)]
*  and this opened the way for Jewish militias to organize their own retaliations. [[02:55:45](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10545.7s)]
*  Now these Zionist militias attacked Arab civilians, and the reports of each side's attacks on the other can hardly be told apart. [[02:55:49](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10549.7s)]
*  Jews were shot and stabbed in the narrow lanes, atrocities were committed by both sides, and some Arab women lying wounded in the fields were seen to have their breasts sliced off by Jewish colonists. [[02:55:56](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10556.7s)]
*  There are vicious people in the world. They exist everywhere, but they tend to just collect like sewer water in conflict regions like this. [[02:56:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10568.7s)]
*  The problem is that when people feel threatened, they lose interest in discerning the intentions of individuals on the other side. [[02:56:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10577.7s)]
*  How nuanced are you really going to get? Think about it. [[02:56:24](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10584.7s)]
*  If a riot occurs and people from the other side beat a 14-year-old Jewish girl to death with rods, [[02:56:27](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10587.7s)]
*  or if you're an Arab who hears about Jewish colonists slicing off the breasts of Arab women, how likely are you to care that it was only a few psychos on the other side doing it? [[02:56:33](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10593.7s)]
*  You're just going to want them all to get out of here. These problems didn't exist before they came. [[02:56:42](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10602.7s)]
*  You know, again, the worst of the worst have a way of dragging conflicts down to their level. [[02:56:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10608.7s)]
*  You see it in just about every single asymmetric and irregular war. [[02:56:53](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10613.7s)]
*  The most ruthless and brutal elements do something that enrages the other side, [[02:56:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10618.7s)]
*  and then the most brutal elements from the other side returns with an atrocity of their own, and that escalates the conflict even more. [[02:57:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10622.7s)]
*  With every new outrage by the other side, the most aggressive, the most militant elements on your side gain more and more followers and seem to make more and more sense. [[02:57:08](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10628.7s)]
*  The riots went on for a week. When it was over, 47 Jews had been killed and 48 Arabs were dead. Hundreds were wounded. [[02:57:17](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10637.7s)]
*  The Jaffa riots sent another shockwave through the British administration and the Zionist movement. [[02:57:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10645.7s)]
*  Only this time some of that shockwave started to be felt in the upper reaches of the British government. [[02:57:30](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10650.7s)]
*  Since the Nebi Musa report had been suppressed, most of the British government continued to believe that things were going well in Palestine. [[02:57:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10656.7s)]
*  When the Jaffa riots broke out, they seemed to come out of the blue for most British officials. [[02:57:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10663.7s)]
*  They were shocked to hear that in the wake of the disturbance, British police found hundreds of rifles, tons of explosives and fuses, and hundreds of bombs which had been smuggled into the country by the Zionists. [[02:57:48](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10668.7s)]
*  They didn't know what to make of that. [[02:57:58](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10678.7s)]
*  The government sent an investigative committee to go look into the incident, and the report it generated just shocked the British officials who received it. [[02:58:01](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10681.7s)]
*  Just like the suppressed Nebi Musa report, the report on the Jaffa riots states that the immediate cause of the violence was the attack on Jews by groups of Arabs. [[02:58:10](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10690.7s)]
*  But also, just like the Nebi Musa report, the committee stated that the more general causes had to do with the Arabs' very real fear that they were being pushed out of their country by the British at the behest of the Zionists. [[02:58:18](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10698.7s)]
*  Now most British officials just did not know what to make of this. [[02:58:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10711.7s)]
*  You have to remember, this is a backwater at the time. It's not the center of geopolitics the way it is today. [[02:58:35](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10715.7s)]
*  Hadn't the British repeatedly said that they had no intention of displacing the Arabs? [[02:58:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10721.7s)]
*  Hadn't the Zionists said all along that they only wished to make a home alongside the Arabs in Palestine? [[02:58:46](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10726.7s)]
*  Why were the Arabs being so paranoid? [[02:58:52](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10732.7s)]
*  Well, the committee said if the Arabs thought Zionism meant losing their homes, it's because that's the message they were getting from the Zionists themselves. [[02:58:55](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10735.7s)]
*  Whatever the British government thought, the Zionists seemed to believe that the British had agreed to help them take Palestine from the Arabs and establish a Jewish state. [[02:59:02](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10742.7s)]
*  Now the High Commissioner Herbert Samuel, if he had any lingering doubts, became firm in his belief that it was madness to hope that the Arabs were ever going to agree to be ruled by European Jews in a Jewish state. [[02:59:11](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10751.7s)]
*  Until now he had kind of hoped, just like Chaim Wiseman had kind of hoped, and he would continue to hope it after this. [[02:59:25](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10765.7s)]
*  He's not in Palestine. He doesn't have to deal with the reality the way Samuel and some others do. [[02:59:31](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10771.7s)]
*  He hoped that the Arabs' nationalism wasn't really that deeply felt. [[02:59:36](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10776.7s)]
*  And that maybe they would eventually give it up when they saw that the British and the Jews would be bringing a lot of money and wealth into the country. [[02:59:41](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10781.7s)]
*  But after Jaffa, he realized that this was never going to happen. [[02:59:47](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10787.7s)]
*  The Arabs' desire for independence was just as strong as the Zionists. [[02:59:51](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6iC9VKpOwsU&t=10791.7s)]
